<p>A general Riemann sum with <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> rectangles that approximates the area under the graph over the <a href="Interval">interval</a> <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c5B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c5D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> above can be described as follows</p>

<h1>Types</h1>
<h2>Left Bounded (LRAM)</h2>
<p>A left bounded Riemann sum is a Riemann sum where the <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D450 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> value is the leftmost point of the partition. In left bounded Riemann sums typically the partitions are equal lengths.</p>

<p>A general left bounded Riemann sum with <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> rectangles over the <a href="Interval">interval</a> <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c5B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c5D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> can be described as follows</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mtext class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c41"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c72"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c65"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c61"></mjx-c></mjx-mtext><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2248"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-munderover space="4"><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.192em; padding-left: 0.51em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-over><mjx-box><mjx-munder><mjx-row><mjx-base><mjx-mo class="mjx-lop"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2211 TEX-S2"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-base></mjx-row><mjx-row><mjx-under style="padding-top: 0.167em; padding-left: 0.086em;"><mjx-TeXAtom size="s" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D458 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-TeXAtom></mjx-under></mjx-row></mjx-munder></mjx-box></mjx-munderover><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D458 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c22C5"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c394"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D458 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Where <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub><mjx-mi TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2026"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub space="2"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> is a partition of <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c5B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-c5D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> and <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c394"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c -0.15em;"><mjx-TeXAtom size="s" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2212"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn <div class="callout" data-callout="note">
<div class="callout-title">
<div class="callout-title-icon">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-pencil"><path d="M17 3a2.85 2.83 0 1 1 4 4L7.5 20.5 2 22l1.5-5.5Z"/><path d="m15 5 4 4"/></svg>
</div>
<div class="callout-title-inner">Note</div>
</div>
<div class="callout-content"><p>The LRAM will <strong>overestimate</strong> if the <a href="Derivative">derivative</a> of the function is less than 0 (the function is decreasing), and will <strong>underestimate</strong> if the <a href="Derivative">derivative</a> of the function is greater than 0 (the function is increasing).</p>
</div></div><h2>Right Bounded (RRAM)</h2>
<p>A right bounded Riemann sum is a Riemann sum where the <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D450 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> value is the rightmost point of the partition. In right bounded Riemann sums typically the partitions are equal lengths.</p>

<p>A general right bounded Riemann sum with <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> rectangles over the <a href="Interval">interval</a> <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c5B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c5D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> can be described as follows</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mtext class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c41"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c72"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c65"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c61"></mjx-c></mjx-mtext><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2248"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-munderover space="4"><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.192em; <p>Where <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub><mjx-mi <div class="callout" data-callout="note">
<div class="callout-title">
<div class="callout-title-icon">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-pencil"><path d="M17 3a2.85 2.83 0 1 1 4 4L7.5 20.5 2 22l1.5-5.5Z"/><path d="m15 5 4 4"/></svg>
</div>
<div class="callout-title-inner">Note</div>
</div>
<div class="callout-content"><p>The RRAM will <strong>underestimate</strong> if the <a href="Derivative">derivative</a> of the function is less than 0 (the function is decreasing), and will <strong>overestimate</strong> if the <a href="Derivative">derivative</a> of the function is greater than 0 (the function is increasing).</p>
</div></div><h2>Middle Bounded (MRAM)</h2>
<p>A middle bounded Riemann sum is a Riemann sum where the <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D450 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> value is the middlemost point of the partition. In middle bounded Riemann sums typically the partitions are equal lengths.</p>

<h2>Trapezoidal Approximation</h2>
<p>The trapezoidal approximation is a Riemann that uses trapezoids instead of rectangles. In trapezoidal Riemann sums typically the partitions are equal lengths. The trapezoidal approximation can be calculated as an average between the <a href="Riemann%20Sum#Left%20Bounded%20(LRAM)">LRAM</a> and <a href="Riemann%20Sum#Right%20Bounded%20(RRAM)">RRAM</a>.</p>
<p>A general trapezoidal approximation with <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> trapezoids over the <a href="Interval">interval</a> <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c5B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c5D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> can be described as follows</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mtext class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c41"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c72"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c65"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c61"></mjx-c></mjx-mtext><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2248"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mfrac space="4"><mjx-frac type="d"><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut type="d"></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mrow><mjx-mtext class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c4C"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c52"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c41"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c4D"></mjx-c></mjx-mtext><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mtext class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c52"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c52"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c41"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c4D"></mjx-c></mjx-mtext></mjx-mrow></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line type="d"></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut type="d"></mjx-dstrut><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-den></mjx-row></mjx-dtable></mjx-dbox></mjx-frac></mjx-mfrac></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Where <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mtext class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c4C"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c52"></mjx-c><mjx-c href="Interval">interval</a> <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c5B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi <div class="callout-title">
<div class="callout-title-icon">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-pencil"><path d="M17 3a2.85 2.83 0 1 1 4 4L7.5 20.5 2 22l1.5-5.5Z"/><path d="m15 5 4 4"/></svg>
</div>
<div class="callout-title-inner">Note</div>
</div>
<div class="callout-content"><p>The trapezoidal approximation will <strong>overestimate</strong> if the <a href="Higher%20Order%20Derivatives">second derivative</a> of the function is greater than 0 (the function is <a href="Concavity#Concave%20Up">concave up</a>), and will <strong>underestimate</strong> if the <a href="Higher%20Order%20Derivatives">second derivative</a> of the function is less than 0 (the function is <a href="Concavity#Concave%20Down">concave down</a>).</p>
